+create_world( levelw, levelh)

+function renderLine( line, pattern)
+    for i=1, strlen(pattern) do
+        local c = strsub( pattern, i, i)
+        if c =="#" then
+            set_stone("st-greenbrown", i-1, line)
+        elseif c =="%" then
+            set_stone("st-invisible", i-1, line)
+            abyss(i-1,line)
+        elseif c == "o" then
+            oxyd( i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "*" then
+            set_stone("st-brownie", i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "F" then
+            set_stone("st-greenbrown", i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "!" then
+            abyss(i-1,line)
+        elseif c == "~" then
+            fill_floor("fl-water", i-1,line, 1,1)
+        elseif c=="z" then
+            set_actor("ac-blackball", i-1,line+.5, {player=0})
+        elseif c == "G" then
+            draw_stones("st-grate1",{i-1,line}, {1,1}, 1)
+        elseif c=="+" then
+            set_stone("st-wood", i-1, line)
+        elseif c=="=" then
+            set_floor("fl-space",i-1,line)
+        elseif c=="A" then
+            if fa==1 then
+                set_floor("fl-bluegreen",i-1,line)
+            elseif fb==1 then
+                set_floor("fl-rough-red",i-1,line)
+            elseif fc==1 then
+                set_floor("fl-sand",i-1,line)
+            elseif fd==1 then
+                set_floor("fl-leaves",i-1,line)
+            end
+        elseif c=="B" then
+            if fa==2 then
+                set_floor("fl-bluegreen",i-1,line)
+            elseif fb==2 then
+                set_floor("fl-rough-red",i-1,line)
+            elseif fc==2 then
+                set_floor("fl-sand",i-1,line)
+            elseif fd==2 then
+                set_floor("fl-leaves",i-1,line)
+            end
+        elseif c=="C" then
+            if fa==3 then
+                set_floor("fl-bluegreen",i-1,line)
+            elseif fb==3 then
+                set_floor("fl-rough-red",i-1,line)
+            elseif fc==3 then
+                set_floor("fl-sand",i-1,line)
+            elseif fd==3 then
+                set_floor("fl-leaves",i-1,line)
+            end
+        elseif c=="D" then
+            if fa==4 then
+                set_floor("fl-bluegreen",i-1,line)
+            elseif fb==4 then
+                set_floor("fl-rough-red",i-1,line)
+            elseif fc==4 then
+                set_floor("fl-sand",i-1,line)
+            elseif fd==4 then
+                set_floor("fl-leaves",i-1,line)
+            end
+        elseif c=="E" then
+            set_floor("fl-sand",i-1,line)
+            set_actor("ac-blackball", i-1,line+.5, {player=0})
+        elseif c=="a" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch1", action="callback", target="funcc1"})
+        elseif c=="b" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch2", action="callback", target="funcc2"})
+        elseif c=="c" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch3", action="callback", target="funcc3"})
+        elseif c=="d" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch4", action="callback", target="funcc4"})
+        elseif c=="e" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch5", action="callback", target="funcc5"})

+        elseif c=="n" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch14", action="callback", target="funcc14"})
+        elseif c=="`" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch15", action="callback", target="funcc15"})
+        elseif c=="p" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch16", action="callback", target="funcc16"})
+        elseif c=="q" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch17", action="callback", target="funcc17"})
+        elseif c=="r" then
+            set_stone("st-fourswitch", i-1,line, {name="switch18", action="callback", target="funcc18"})
+        elseif c == "d" then --1-d
+            set_floor("fl-gradient",  i-1,  line, {type=1})
+        elseif c == "u" then --2-u
+            set_floor("fl-gradient",  i-1,  line, {type=2})
+        elseif c == "U" then --2-u
+            set_floor("fl-gradient",  i-1,  line, {type=2})
+            set_actor("ac-bug",i-.5,line+.5,{mouseforce=0,player=1})
+        elseif c=="1" then
+            set_stone("st-door_b",i-1,line,{name="door1"})
+        elseif c=="2" then
+            set_stone("st-door_b",i-1,line,{name="door2"})
+        elseif c=="3" then
+            doorv( i-1,line, {name="door3"})
+        elseif c=="4" then
+            doorv( i-1,line, {name="door4"})
+        elseif c=="5" then
+            set_item("it-trigger", i-1,line, {invisible=1,action="callback", target="funccblock1"})
+        elseif c=="6" then
+            set_item("it-trigger", i-1,line, {invisible=1,action="callback", target="funccblock2"})
+        elseif c=="7" then
+            set_item("it-trigger", i-1,line, {invisible=1,action="callback", target="funccblock3"})
+        elseif c=="8" then
+            set_item("it-trigger", i-1,line, {invisible=1,action="callback", target="funccblock4"})
+        elseif c=="9" then

+        elseif c=="0" then

+        elseif c=="H" then

+    end    
+end

+end

+f1=1
+function funcc1()
+    f1=f1+1
+    if f1==1 then
+        floor1(20)
+    elseif f1==2 then
+        floor2(20)
+    elseif f1==3 then
+        floor3(20)
+    elseif f1==4 then
+        floor4(20)
+        f1=0
+    end
+    funcc19()
+end

+f2=1

+function renderLine( line, pattern)
+    for i=1, strlen(pattern) do
+        local c = strsub( pattern, i, i)
+        if c =="#" then
+            set_stone( "st-greenbrown", i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "o" then
+            oxyd( i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "i" then
+            set_stone( "st-invisible", i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "h" then
+            set_item("it-trigger", i-1,line, {action="openclose",target="door1"})
+        elseif c == "H" then
+            set_stone("st-door", i-1, line , {name="door1", type="v"})
+        elseif c == "+" then
+            set_stone("st-wood", i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "*" then
+            set_stone("st-brownie", i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "g" then
+            draw_stones("st-grate1",{i-1,line}, {1,1}, 1)
+        elseif c == "a" then
+            set_stone("st-bolder", i-1,line, {direction=NORTH})

+            set_stone("st-bolder", i-1,line, {direction=EAST})
+        elseif c == "c" then
+            set_stone("st-bolder", i-1,line, {direction=WEST})
+        elseif c == "d" then
+            set_stone("st-bolder", i-1,line, {direction=SOUTH})
+        elseif c == "1" then
+            oneway(i-1,line, enigma.NORTH)
+        elseif c == "4" then
+            oneway(i-1,line, enigma.SOUTH)
+        elseif c == "3" then
+            oneway(i-1,line, enigma.WEST)
+        elseif c == "2" then
+            oneway(i-1,line, enigma.EAST)
+        elseif c == "~" then
+            fill_floor("fl-water", i-1,line, 1,1)
+        elseif c == "!" then

+function renderLine( line, pattern)
+    for i=1, strlen(pattern) do
+        local c = strsub( pattern, i, i)
+        if c =="#" then
+            set_stone("st-greenbrown",i-1,line)
+        elseif c == "o" then
+            oxyd( i-1, line)
+        elseif c == "s" then
+            set_stone("st-stoneimpulse",i-1,line)
+        elseif c == "*" then
+            set_stone("st-brownie", i-1, line)
+         elseif c == "d" then
+            set_stone("st-bolder", i-1,line, {direction=SOUTH})
+        elseif c == "u" then
+            set_stone("st-bolder", i-1,line, {direction=NORTH})
+        elseif c == "l" then
+            set_stone("st-bolder", i-1,line, {direction=WEST})
+        elseif c == "!" then
+            set_floor("fl-water",i-1,line)
+        elseif c == "z" then    
+            set_actor("ac-blackball" ,i-1, line, {player=0})
+        end
+    end
+end

+-- Code
+homex=63.5
+homey=38.5

+finishy=90.5
+xx=0
+
+function start_timing()
+    if xx == 0 then
+        set_item("it-wormhole", 136, 90, {targetx=175.5, targety=90.5})
+        xx=1
+    else
+        enigma.KillItem(136,90)
+        enigma.KillStone(135,89)
+        enigma.KillStone(136,89)
+        enigma.KillStone(137,89)
+        enigma.KillStone(135,90)
+        enigma.KillStone(137,90)
+        enigma.KillStone(135,91)
+        enigma.KillStone(136,91)
+        enigma.KillStone(137,91)
+        SendMessage("timer1","off")
+    end
+end
+
+function puzzle1()
+    puzzle({" #     ", 
+          "###### ", 
+          " ## ###", 
+          " ##### ", 
+          "    #  "}, {41,39}, "redpuzzle", "permutation")
+end
+
+function refill()
+    local water = 0
+    local floor = enigma.GetFloor(131, 18)
+    local water1 = false
+    local water2 = false
+    local water3 = false
+    if floor ~= nil then
+        if GetKind(floor) == "fl-water" then
+            water = water + 1
+            water1 = true
+        end
+    end
+    floor = enigma.GetFloor(131, 19)
+    if floor ~= nil then
+        if GetKind(floor) == "fl-water" then
+            water = water + 1
+            water2 = true
+        end
+    end
+    floor = enigma.GetFloor(132, 19)
+    if floor ~= nil then
+        if GetKind(floor) == "fl-water" then
+            water = water + 1
+            water3 = true
+        end
+    end
+    if water > 0 then
+        local obj = enigma.GetItem(132, 18)
+        local didFill = 0
+        if obj == nil then
+            if water == 3 then
+                set_item("it-document", 132, 18, {text="text13"})
+            end
+        else
+            if GetKind(obj) == "it-extinguisher_empty" then
+                set_item("it-extinguisher_medium", 132, 18, {})
+                water = water -1
+                didFill = 1
+            else
+                if GetKind(obj) == "it-extinguisher_medium" and water > 1 then
+                    set_item("it-extinguisher", 132, 18, {})
+                    water = water - 2
+                    didFill = 2
+                end
+            end
+        end
+        if didFill >= 1 and water1 then
+            set_floor("fl-swamp", 131, 18, {})
+            didFill = didFill - 1
+        end
+        if didFill >= 1 and water2 then
+            set_floor("fl-swamp", 131, 19, {})
+            didFill = didFill - 1
+        end
+        if didFill >= 1 and water3 then
+            set_floor("fl-swamp", 132, 19, {})
+        end
+    end
+end
+

+<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" standalone="no" ?>
+<el:level xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" xsi:schemaLocation="http://enigma-game.org/schema/level/1 level.xsd" xmlns:el="http://enigma-game.org/schema/level/1">
+  <el:protected >
+    <el:info el:type="level">
+      <el:identity el:title="Restless Meditation" el:subtitle="Caution - Quick Sand!" el:id="20070623ral914"/>
+      <el:version el:score="1" el:release="1" el:revision="$Revision: 77 $" el:status="released"/>
+      <el:author  el:name="Ronald Lamprecht" el:email="ral at users.berlios.de"/>
+      <el:copyright>Copyright © 2006 Ronald Lamprecht</el:copyright>
+      <el:license el:type="GPL v2.0 or above" el:open="true"/>
+      <el:compatibility el:enigma="1.00">
+      </el:compatibility>
+      <el:modes el:easy="true" el:single="true" el:network="false"/>
+      <el:comments>
+        <el:code>Lua 5.1</el:code>
+      </el:comments>
+      <el:score el:easy="0:26" el:difficult="0:47"/>
+    </el:info>
+    <el:luamain><![CDATA[
+enigma.ConserveLevel = TRUE
+math_floor = floor
+
+set_oxyd = oxyd
+
+function oxyd( x, y, tiles )
+    return set_oxyd( x, y )
+end
+
+function nothing(x, y, tiles)
+    -- create nothing
+end
+
+function horizontal_bolder(x,y,tiles)
+    if random() >= 0.5 then
+        return set_stone( "st-bolder-w", x, y )
+    else
+        return set_stone( "st-bolder-e", x, y )
+    end
+end
+
+function vertical_bolder(x,y,tiles)
+    if random() >= 0.5 then
+        return set_stone( "st-bolder-n", x, y )
+    else
+        return set_stone( "st-bolder-s", x, y )
+    end
+end
+
+function checkerboard_floor( type1, type2, attribs1, attribs2 )
+    return function( x, y, tiles )
+        if mod(x,2) == mod(y,2) then
+            return set_floor( type1, x, y, attribs1 or {} )
+        else
+            return set_floor( type2, x, y, attribs2 or {} )
+        end
+    end
+end
+
+function floor( floor_type, attribs )
+    return function( x, y, tiles )
+        return set_floor( floor_type, x, y, attribs or {} )
+    end
+end
+
+function stone( stone_type, attribs )
+    return function( x, y, tiles )
+        return set_stone( stone_type, x, y, attribs or {} )
+    end
+end
+
+function item( item_type, attribs )
+    return function( x, y, tiles )
+        return set_item( item_type, x, y, attribs or {} )
+    end
+end
+
+function actor( actor_type, attribs )
+    return function( x, y, tiles )
+        return set_actor( actor_type, x+0.5, y+0.5, attribs or {} )
+    end
+end
+
+function gradient( gradient_type )
+    return function( x, y, tiles )
+        return set_floor( "fl-gradient", x, y, {type=gradient_type} )
+    end
+end
+
+function inherit(tile_type)
+    return function( x, y, tiles )
+        return create_tile( tiles, x, y, tile_type )
+    end
+end
+
+function group( array, constructor )
+    return function( x, y, tiles )
+        object = constructor( x, y, tiles )
+        tinsert( array, object )
+        return object
+    end
+end
+
+function difficulty( d, constructor )
+    if options.Difficulty == d then
+        return constructor
+    else
+        return nothing
+    end
+end
+
+function create_world_from_map( tiles, map )
+    create_world( strlen(map[1]), getn(map) )
+
+    for y = 1,getn(map) do
+        local line = map[y]
+        for x = 1,strlen(line) do
+            local tile = strchar(strbyte(line,x))
+            create_tile( tiles, x-1, y-1, tile )
+        end
+    end
+end
+
+function create_tile( tiles, x, y, tile_type )
+    local constructors = tiles[tile_type]
+
+    if constructors then
+    for i = 1,getn(constructors) do
+        constructors[i](x,y,tiles)
+    end
+    else
+    error("invalid tile identifier " .. tile_type )
+    end
+end
+
+tiles = {}
+tiles[" "] = {floor("fl-swamp")}
+tiles["#"] = {inherit(" "), stone("st-wood")}
+if difficult then
+  enigma.SwampSinkSpeed = 2.5
+  tiles["."] = {inherit(" "), item("it-hollow")}
+  tiles["1"] = {inherit(" "), actor("ac-whiteball-small", {essential=1, player=0, controllers=1})}
+  tiles["*"] = tiles[" "]
+  tiles["2"] = tiles[" "]
+else
+  enigma.SwampSinkSpeed = 1.5
+  tiles["*"] = {inherit(" "), item("it-hollow")}
+  tiles["2"] = {inherit(" "), actor("ac-whiteball-small", {essential=1, player=0, controllers=1})}
+  tiles["."] = tiles[" "]
+  tiles["1"] = tiles[" "]
+end
+
+create_world_from_map( tiles, {
+"####################",
+"#                  #",
+"# .              . #",
+"#  *            *  #",
+"#                  #",
+"#      2    2      #",
+"#       1111       #",
+"#      2    2      #",
+"#                  #",
+"#  *            *  #",
+"# .              . #",
+"#                  #",
+"####################"
+})
+
+    ]]></el:luamain>

+        <el:english el:translate="true"/>
+        <el:translation el:lang="de">Ruhelose Meditation</el:translation>
